is a very simple Crazy Eights-style card game, with a bunch of strategy cards thrown in to make it interesting.\r\n\r\nBrace yourself for the fast paced Ho-Uno card game. The idea of the game is to get to your last card, shout Ho-Uno before another player realises you didn‚Äôt, and then attempt to play your last card on your turn to win the round. The player to use up the last card wins the round and is scored based on the cards left in their opponent‚Äôs hand.\r\n\r\nEach player is dealt 7 cards with the remaining ones placed face down to form a draw pile. The top card of the draw pile is turned over to begin a discard pile.\r\n\r\nThe objective of the game is to be the first player to shout Ho-Uno. Points are scored by ridding yourself of all the cards in your hand before your opponents.
